) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[BookId], [b].[BorrowDate], [b].[CreatedAt], [b].[CreatedBy], [b].[Deleted], [b].[IsReturned], [b].[ReturnDate], [b].[UpdatedAt], [b].[UpdatedBy], [b].[UserId], [t1].[Id] AS [Id0], [t1].[AuthorId], [t1].[CategoryId], [t1].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [t1].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy0], [t1].[Deleted] AS [Deleted0], [t1].[ISBN], [t1].[IsAvailable], [t1].[PublishDate], [t1].[Title], [t1].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0], [t1].[UpdatedBy] AS [UpdatedBy0]

    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [b0].[Id], [b0].[AuthorId], [b0].[CategoryId], [b0].[CreatedAt], [b0].[CreatedBy], [b0].[Deleted], [b0].[ISBN], [b0].[IsAvailable], [b0].[PublishDate], [b0].[Title], [b0].[UpdatedAt], [b0].[UpdatedBy]

    ) AS [t1] ON [b].[BookId] = [t1].[Id]
